## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population P, which is the canonical form of population dynamics ODEs. Classical models include density-dependent growth (logistic, Gompertz, Allee) and potentially time-varying growth rates.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent unlimited growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth, common in tumor/microbial growth)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population threshold)
- Weak Allee effect: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 * (1 - c2 * P) (reduced per-capita growth at low density)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) * c3 (flexible asymmetric growth curve)
- Beverton-Holt continuous form: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (density-dependent with hyperbolic saturation)
- Logistic with time-varying rate: dP_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) * P * (1 - c2 * P) (seasonally or temporally modulated growth)
- Power-law growth: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 (allometric/fractal growth scaling)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolism-catabolism balance)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (growth with constant removal rate)
- Time-dependent exponential: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (exponentially changing environment)
- Quadratic density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 (simplest polynomial density-dependent model)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear proportionality to P (dP_dt ~ c*P) indicates density-independent exponential growth regime
- Quadratic term in P (dP_dt ~ c0*P - c1*P^2) signals logistic-type carrying capacity limitation
- Logarithmic coupling with P (dP_dt ~ P*log(P)) suggests Gompertz-type growth with multiplicative stochastic origins
- Cubic polynomial in P (dP_dt ~ P*(P-a)*(K-P)) indicates Allee effect with both lower and upper population bounds
- Rational dependence on P (dP_dt ~ P/(1+c*P)) suggests resource competition with handling time or interference
- Fractional power of P (dP_dt ~ P^(2/3)) often arises from surface-area-to-volume scaling in organism growth
- Explicit time dependence combined with P suggests non-autonomous dynamics like seasonal forcing or environmental drift
- Difference of power laws (dP_dt ~ P^a - P^b) reflects competing biological processes with different allometric scaling
- Product P*(1 - c*P) structure universally indicates negative feedback from intraspecific competition at carrying capacity

**Candidate 4:** `P²c0/(Pc1+c2) + P²c3*exp(c4*t)/(Pc1+c2) + Pc5/(Pc1+c2) + Pc6*exp(c4*t)/(Pc1+c2) + c7*t/(Pc1+c2) + c8/(Pc1+c2)`

= `[P²c0 + Pc6*exp(c4*t)]/(Pc1+c2)`

But GT has `P*exp(αt)` NOT divided by `(Pc1+c2)`. So this doesn't match unless c1=0, making denominator c2, which gives `P²c0/c2 + Pc6*exp(c4*t)/c2` — but then `P²c0/c2` is just `P²` times a constant, not `P²/(aP+b)`. No match.

**Candidate 44:** `P²c0/(Pc1+c2) + P²c3*exp(c4*t)/(Pc1+c2) + Pc5/(Pc1+c2) + Pc6*exp(c4*t)/(Pc1+c2) + c7/(Pc1+c2)`

For this to match GT = `αP*exp(βt) + γP²/(δP+ε)`, I need:
`Pc6*exp(c4*t)/(Pc1+c2) = αP*exp(βt)` → requires `Pc1+c2` to be constant, meaning c1=0. Then denominator = c2.

With c1=0: `[P²c0 + Pc5 + Pc6*exp(c4*t) + c7]/c2 = (c0/c2)P² + (c5/c2)P + (c6/c2)P*exp(c4*t) + c7/c2`

This gives `P²*(const) + P*(const) + P*exp(c4*t)*(const) + const`, which is NOT `P²/(aP+b)`. No match.

**Candidate 9:** `Pc0 + Pc1*exp(c2*t) + Pc3/(Pc4+c5) + c6*exp(c7/P) + c8/(Pc4+c5)`

= `Pc0 + Pc1*exp(c2*t) + (Pc3+c8)/(Pc4+c5)`

Setting c0=0, c8=0: `Pc1*exp(c2*t) + Pc3/(Pc4+c5)`

Now `Pc3/(Pc4+c5) = c3*P/(c4*P+c5)`. But GT needs `P²/(aP+b)`. These differ: `P/(aP+b)` vs `P²/(aP+b)`. Not the same.

**Candidate 8:** `Pc0 + Pc1*exp(c2*t) + Pc3/(Pc4+1) + P^c5*c6`

Setting c5=2, c0=0: `Pc1*exp(c2*t) + Pc3/(Pc4+1) + c6*P²`

**Candidate 33:** `P²c0/(Pc1+1) + P²c2*exp(c3*t)/(Pc1+1) + Pc4*exp(c3*t)/(Pc1+1)`

Expanding numerator: `c0*c4*P²*exp(-c1*t) + c0*c5*P*exp(-c1*t) + c2*P²`

So GT numerator = `c2*P² + c0*c4*P²*exp(-c1*t) + c0*c5*P*exp(-c1*t)`

Candidate 4 numerator = `c0*P² + c3*P²*exp(c4*t) + c5*P + c6*P*exp(c4*t) + c7*t + c8`

Set c7=0, c8=0: `c0_P² + c3_P²*exp(c4_t) + c5_P + c6_P*exp(c4_t)`

This matches the GT numerator structure! We need:
- P² coefficient: c0_cand = c2_GT (constant) ✓
- P²*exp: c3_cand*exp(c4_cand*t) matches c0_GT*c4_GT*exp(-c1_GT*t) ✓ (set c4_cand = -c1_GT)
- P coefficient: c5_cand = 0 (but GT has no standalone P term without exp... wait)

GT numerator: `c2*P² + c0*c4*P²*exp(-c1*t) + c0*c5*P*exp(-c1*t)`

Candidate numerator (with c7=c8=0): `c0'*P² + c3'*P²*exp(c4'*t) + c5'*P + c6'*P*exp(c4'*t)`

GT has no standalone P term (without exp), so set c5'=0. Then:
- c0' matches c2_GT ✓
- c3'*exp(c4'*t) matches c0_GT*c4_GT*exp(-c1_GT*t) ✓
- c6'*exp(c4'*t) matches c0_GT*c5_GT*exp(-c1_GT*t) ✓

This works! **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 5: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3/(c4*t+c5) + c6*exp(c7/P) + c8/(c4*t+c5)`
Has time-dependent rational terms and exp(c7/P). Set c3=0, c8=0, c6=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t)`. Missing rational P term. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 6: `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2*log(c3/(P+c4)+1) + P*c5 + P*c6*exp(c1*t) + P^c7*c8`
Has log term. Set c2=0: `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c5 + P*c6*exp(c1*t) + P^c7*c8`. 
We need P²/(linear P). P^c7*c8 is a power law, not rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 7: `P²*c0 + P²*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4/(P*c5+c6) + P*c7 + c8/(P*c5+c6)`
Combine: `P²*(c0+c1) + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*(c7) + [P*c4+c8]/(P*c5+c6)`

The rational part: `(P*c4+c8)/(P*c5+c6)`. We need P²/(linear P). 

Can we combine P²*(c0+c1) with the rational part? Let's put over common denominator:
`[P²*(c0+c1)*(P*c5+c6) + P*c4+c8]/(P*c5+c6)`

This gives P³ terms in numerator, which GT doesn't have. Unless c0+c1=0.

If c0+c1=0: `P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c7 + (P*c4+c8)/(P*c5+c6)`

We need `(P*c4+c8)/(P*c5+c6)` to equal `P²/(aP+b)` plus possibly absorbing P*c7.

Actually: `P*c7 + (P*c4+c8)/(P*c5+c6)` = `[P*c7*(P*c5+c6) + P*c4+c8]/(P*c5+c6)` = `[c7*c5*P² + (c7*c6+c4)*P + c8]/(P*c5+c6)`

For this to equal `αP²/(βP+γ)`, we need c7*c6+c4=0 and c8=0.

Then: `c7*c5*P²/(P*c5+c6)`. This is exactly `P²` times a constant over (linear in P). ✓

So: total = `P*c2*exp(c3*t) + c7*c5*P²/(P*c5+c6)` which matches GT structure! **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 8: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3/(P*c4+1) + P^c5*c6`
`P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3/(P*c4+1) + P^c5*c6`

We need P²/(linear P). The term P*c3/(P*c4+1) = c3*P/(c4*P+1). 

Can we combine P*c0 with P*c3/(P*c4+1)?
`P*c0 + P*c3/(P*c4+1) = [P*c0*(P*c4+1) + P*c3]/(P*c4+1) = [c0*c4*P² + (c0+c3)*P]/(P*c4+1)`

For this to be P²/(linear P), need c0+c3=0, giving `c0*c4*P²/(P*c4+1)`.

Then remaining: `P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c5*c6`. Set c6=0: `P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c0*c4*P²/(c4*P+1)`.

This matches GT! But wait, can we also keep P^c5*c6? We'd need c6=0 since GT has no extra power law term.

So: `c0*c4*P²/(c4*P+1) + P*c1*exp(c2*t)` matches GT. **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 9: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3/(P*c4+c5) + c6*exp(c7/P) + c8/(P*c4+c5)`
Set c6=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3/(P*c4+c5) + c8/(P*c4+c5)`
= `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + (P*c3+c8)/(P*c4+c5)`

Combine P*c0 with rational: `[P*c0*(P*c4+c5) + P*c3+c8]/(P*c4+c5) = [c0*c4*P² + (c0*c5+c3)*P + c8]/(P*c4+c5)`

For P²/(linear P): need c0*c5+c3=0 and c8=0.
Then: `c0*c4*P²/(P*c4+c5) + P*c1*exp(c2*t)`. **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 10: `P²*c0 + P²*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4 + P*c5/(P*c6+c7)`
= `P²*(c0+c1) + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4 + P*c5/(P*c6+c7)`

Combine P²*(c0+c1) + P*c4 + P*c5/(P*c6+c7):
Over common denominator: `[P²*(c0+c1)*(P*c6+c7) + P*c4*(P*c6+c7) + P*c5]/(P*c6+c7)`

This gives P³ unless c0+c1=0.

If c0+c1=0: `P*c4 + P*c5/(P*c6+c7)` = `[P*c4*(P*c6+c7) + P*c5]/(P*c6+c7)` = `[c4*c6*P² + (c4*c7+c5)*P]/(P*c6+c7)`

For P²/(linear P): need c4*c7+c5=0.
Then: `c4*c6*P²/(P*c6+c7) + P*c2*exp(c3*t)`. **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 11: `P²*c0 + P²*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4 + P*c5/(P*c6+1)`
Same as 10 but with denominator P*c6+1 (c7 fixed to 1). Same analysis:
Set c0+c1=0, c4+c5/(P*c6+1) combined:
`[c4*c6*P² + (c4+c5)*P]/(P*c6+1)`. Need c4+c5=0.
Then: `c4*c6*P²/(P*c6+1) + P*c2*exp(c3*t)`. 

GT denominator is 9.871*P+1, so c6=9.871 and denominator is 9.871P+1. The "1" is fixed here. ✓ **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 12: `P*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2*(c3+t)^c4 + P*c5/(P*c6+c7)`
Has (c3+t)^c4 term. Set c4=0: P*c2*1 = P*c2. Then: `P*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c5/(P*c6+c7)`.
Combine P*c2 + P*c5/(P*c6+c7) = [P*c2*(P*c6+c7)+P*c5]/(P*c6+c7) = [c2*c6*P²+(c2*c7+c5)*P]/(P*c6+c7).
Set c2*c7+c5=0: `c2*c6*P²/(P*c6+c7) + P*c0*exp(c1*t)`. **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 13: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4 + P^c5*c6*log(c7*t+1) + c8*exp(c9/P)`
Set c6=0, c8=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4`. Power law, not rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 14: `P*P^c0*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(c4*t) + P^c0*c5 + P^c6*c7`
= `P^(1+c0)*c1 + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(c4*t) + P^c0*c5 + P^c6*c7`
Power laws, no rational function of P. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 15: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*exp(c6/P)`
Set c3=0, c5=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t)`. Missing rational term. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 16: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(c4/P) + c5*t + c6`
Set c3=0, c5=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c6`. Missing rational term. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 17: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*t/(c4*t+c5) + c6/(c4*t+c5) + c7*exp(c8/P)`
Time-dependent rational terms, not P-dependent rational. Set c3=0, c6=0, c7=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t)`. Missing rational P term. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 18: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4 + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*t+1)+c8)`
Set c5=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4`. Power law, not rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 19: `P²*c0*exp(c1*t)/(P+c2) + P²*c3/(P+c2) + P*c4/(P+c2) + P*c5*exp(c1*t)/(P+c2) + c6*t/(P+c2)`
Over common denominator (P+c2):
Numerator: `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P²*c3 + P*c4 + P*c5*exp(c1*t) + c6*t`

Need c6=0 (to eliminate t), c4=0 (to eliminate standalone P).
Then: `[P²*c3 + P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c5*exp(c1*t)]/(P+c2)`
= `[P²*c3 + (P²*c0+P*c5)*exp(c1*t)]/(P+c2)`

GT: `[c2_GT*P² + (c0_GT*c4_GT*P² + c0_GT*c5_GT*P)*exp(-c1_GT*t)]/(c4_GT*P+c5_GT)`

The denominator here is (P+c2) which has leading coefficient 1 for P. GT denominator is c4*P+c5 = 9.871P+1. We can write (P+c2) = (P+c2), and GT denominator = 9.871*(P + 1/9.871). So we'd need to factor out 9.871 from GT denominator and absorb into numerator constants. That's fine since all numerator constants are free.

Matching structure:
- P²*c3 ↔ (c2_GT/c4_GT)*P² ✓ (absorbing the 9.871 factor)
- P²*c0 ↔ (c0_GT*c4_GT/c4_GT_denom) = c0_GT ✓
- P*c5 ↔ c0_GT*c5_GT/c4_GT_denom ✓
- exp(c1*t) ↔ exp(-c1_GT*t) ✓

This works! **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 20: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4*log(c5*t+1) + c6*exp(c7/P)`
Set c4=0, c6=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t)`. Missing rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 21: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(c4/P) + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*t+1)+c8)`

### Candidate 22: `P*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5/(P*c6+c7)`
= `P*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5/(P*c6+c7)`

Set c3=0. Then: `P*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + c5/(P*c6+c7)`.
Combine P*c2 + c5/(P*c6+c7) = [P*c2*(P*c6+c7)+c5]/(P*c6+c7) = [c2*c6*P²+c2*c7*P+c5]/(P*c6+c7).
For P²/(linear P): need c2*c7+0=0... wait, need c2*c7*P+c5=0 for all P. That requires c2*c7=0 AND c5=0.

If c5=0 and c2*c7=0: either c2=0 (loses P² term) or c7=0 (denominator becomes P*c6, giving P²*c2*c6/(P*c6) = c2*P, just linear).

Hmm, let me reconsider. We need the rational part to be P²/(linear P). If c7≠0:
[c2*c6*P² + c2*c7*P + c5]/(P*c6+c7). We need this to equal αP²/(βP+γ). That means c2*c7*P+c5 must be zero, requiring c2*c7=0 and c5=0. If c2=0, no P² term. If c7=0, denominator is c6*P.

Actually wait - GT has P²/(9.871P+1). The coefficient of P in numerator doesn't have to be zero if we allow the full rational function. But GT's rational part is exactly P²/(9.871P+1) = 0.3156*P²/(9.871P+1). There's no P term in the numerator.

So we need c2*c7=0 and c5=0. If c7=0: denominator = P*c6, rational part = c2*P. Not P²/(linear P).

So this can't match. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 23: `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(c1*t) + P^c4*c5*t^c6 + c7`
Set c5=0, c7=0: `P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P*c2 + P*c3*exp(c1*t)` = `(P²*c0+P*c3)*exp(c1*t) + P*c2`. This is polynomial in P times exp, not rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 24: `P*c0 + P^c1*c2*t^c3 + P^c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7`
Set c2=0 (or c3 to eliminate t dependence... actually t^c3 with c3=0 gives 1): 
If c3=0: `P*c0 + P^c1*c2 + P^c4*c5*exp(c6*t) + c7`. Power laws, not rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 25: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6*exp(c7/P)`
Set c6=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4*exp(c5*t)`. 
Set c5=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4`. Power law, not rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 26: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4 + c5*exp(P^c6*c7)`
exp(P^c6*c7) is exponential of power of P. Set c5=0: power law remains. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 27: `P²*c0/(P*c1+1) + P²*c2*exp(c3*t)/(P*c1+1) + P*c4/(P*c1+1) + P*c5*exp(c3*t)/(P*c1+1) + P*c6/(P*c1+1)`

Over common denominator (P*c1+1):
`[P²*c0 + P²*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4 + P*c5*exp(c3*t) + P*c6]/(P*c1+1)`
= `[P²*c0 + P*(c4+c6) + (P²*c2+P*c5)*exp(c3*t)]/(P*c1+1)`

Set c4+c6=0: `[P²*c0 + (P²*c2+P*c5)*exp(c3*t)]/(P*c1+1)`

GT numerator (over 9.871P+1): `0.3156*P² + (0.3156*9.871*P² + 0.3156*1*P)*exp(-0.0541*t)`

Wait, let me recompute GT. GT = c0*P*exp(-c1*t) + c2*P²/(c4*P+c5)

Over common denominator (c4*P+c5):
= [c0*P*exp(-c1*t)*(c4*P+c5) + c2*P²]/(c4*P+c5)
= [c0*c4*P²*exp(-c1*t) + c0*c5*P*exp(-c1*t) + c2*P²]/(c4*P+c5)
= [c2*P² + (c0*c4*P² + c0*c5*P)*exp(-c1*t)]/(c4*P+c5)

Candidate 27 (with c4+c6=0): `[P²*c0' + (P²*c2'+P*c5')*exp(c3'*t)]/(P*c1'+1)`

Denominator: P*c1'+1. GT denominator: c4*P+c5 = 9.871P+1. So c1'=9.871. ✓

Numerator matching:
- P²*c0' = c2_GT*P²/1 (since we factored out nothing from denominator) → c0' = c2_GT/1... wait, the denominators already match (both have coefficient 1 for constant term).

Actually GT denominator = 9.871P+1, candidate denominator = c1'*P+1. Set c1'=9.871. Then:

P²*c0' ↔ c2_GT*P² → c0' = 0.3156 ✓
P²*c2' ↔ c0_GT*c4_GT = 0.3156*9.871 → c2' = 3.115 ✓
P*c5' ↔ c0_GT*c5_GT = 0.3156*1 → c5' = 0.3156 ✓
c3' = -c1_GT = -0.0541 ✓

**[MATCH]**

### Candidate 28: `P^(1/3)*c0 + P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4/(P*c5+c6) + c7/(P*c5+c6)`
Has P^(1/3) term. Set c0=0: `P*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + (P*c4+c7)/(P*c5+c6)`.
Combine P*c1 + (P*c4+c7)/(P*c5+c6) = [P*c1*(P*c5+c6)+P*c4+c7]/(P*c5+c6) = [c1*c5*P²+(c1*c6+c4)*P+c7]/(P*c5+c6).

### Candidate 29: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4*sin(c5*t+c6) + c7*exp(c8/P)`

### Candidate 30: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3*log(1+c4/P) + c5*exp(c6/P)`
P*c3*log(1+c4/P). For P≥0, log(1+c4/P) is not a rational function. It's a transcendental function. Cannot equal P²/(linear P). Set c5=0: still has log term. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 31: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3/(P*c4+c5) + c6*exp(c7/P)`
Set c6=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3/(P*c4+c5)`.

Set c0*c5+c3=0: `c0*c4*P²/(P*c4+c5) + P*c1*exp(c2*t)`. **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 32: `P²*c0*exp(c1*t)/(P+c2) + P²*c3/(P+c2) + P*c4*exp(c1*t)/(P+c2)`
Over (P+c2): `[P²*c0*exp(c1*t) + P²*c3 + P*c4*exp(c1*t)]/(P+c2)`
= `[P²*c3 + (P²*c0+P*c4)*exp(c1*t)]/(P+c2)`

Same structure as GT. Denominator P+c2 can match c4_GT*P+c5_GT by absorbing the factor into numerator constants (since P+c2 = (1/9.871)*(9.871P+9.871c2), set c2=1/9.871).

Wait, GT denominator is 9.871P+1. Candidate denominator is P+c2. These differ by a factor of 9.871: 9.871P+1 = 9.871*(P+1/9.871). So P+c2 with c2=1/9.871 gives P+0.1013. Then 9.871*(P+0.1013) = 9.871P+1. The factor 9.871 gets absorbed into numerator constants.

So: `[P²*c3 + (P²*c0+P*c4)*exp(c1*t)]/(P+c2)` with c2=1/9.871.

Matching to GT (divided by 9.871): `[0.03197*P² + (0.03197*P²+0.03197*P)*exp(-0.0541*t)]/(P+0.1013)`

Hmm, let me just verify the structure matches:
- P²*c3 ↔ constant*P² ✓
- P²*c0*exp(c1*t) ↔ constant*P²*exp(αt) ✓
- P*c4*exp(c1*t) ↔ constant*P*exp(αt) ✓

All three terms present. **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 33: `P²*c0/(P*c1+1) + P²*c2*exp(c3*t)/(P*c1+1) + P*c4*exp(c3*t)/(P*c1+1)`
Over (P*c1+1): `[P²*c0 + P²*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4*exp(c3*t)]/(P*c1+1)`
= `[P²*c0 + (P²*c2+P*c4)*exp(c3*t)]/(P*c1+1)`

Same structure as GT! **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 34: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(c4/P) + c5*log(P^c6*c7+1)`

### Candidate 39: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(c4/P) + c5/(P*c6+c7)`
Set c3=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c5/(P*c6+c7)`.
Combine P*c0 + c5/(P*c6+c7) = [P*c0*(P*c6+c7)+c5]/(P*c6+c7) = [c0*c6*P²+c0*c7*P+c5]/(P*c6+c7).
For P²/(linear P): need c0*c7*P+c5=0 → c0*c7=0 and c5=0.
If c0=0: no P² term. If c7=0: denominator = P*c6, rational = c0*P + c5/(P*c6). Still not right.
If c5=0 and c0*c7=0 and c0≠0: c7=0, denominator = c6*P, rational = c0*c6*P²/(c6*P) = c0*P. Just linear.

**[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 40: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(P*c4) + c5*exp(c6/P)`
Set c3=0, c5=0: missing rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 41: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4 + c5*exp(c6/P)`
Set c5=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4`. Power law, not rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 42: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3 + P^c4*c5 + c6*exp(c7/P)`
Set c6=0: `P*(c0+c3) + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c4*c5`. Power law, not rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 43: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4*exp(c5*t) + P^c6*c7`
Power laws and exponentials. No rational function possible. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 44: `P²*c0/(P*c1+c2) + P²*c3*exp(c4*t)/(P*c1+c2) + P*c5/(P*c1+c2) + P*c6*exp(c4*t)/(P*c1+c2) + c7/(P*c1+c2)`
Over (P*c1+c2): `[P²*c0 + P²*c3*exp(c4*t) + P*c5 + P*c6*exp(c4*t) + c7]/(P*c1+c2)`

GT numerator: `c2_GT*P² + (c0_GT*c4_GT*P² + c0_GT*c5_GT*P)*exp(-c1_GT*t)`

Set c5=0, c7=0: `[P²*c0 + (P²*c3+P*c6)*exp(c4*t)]/(P*c1+c2)`. Matches GT structure! **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 45: Same as 44 but with extra terms P*c6/(P*c1+c2) and c9/(P*c1+c2).
Over (P*c1+c2): `[P²*c0 + P²*c3*exp(c4*t) + P*c5 + P*c6 + P*c7*exp(c4*t) + c8 + c9]/(P*c1+c2)`
= `[P²*c0 + P*(c5+c6) + (c8+c9) + (P²*c3+P*c7)*exp(c4*t)]/(P*c1+c2)`

Set c5+c6=0, c8+c9=0: matches GT. **[MATCH]**

### Candidate 46: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P^c3*c4*t^c5 + c6`
Power law * power of t. Set c4=0, c6=0: missing rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 47-54: All have transcendental terms (sin, log, exp(1/P)) that can be zeroed, but then missing rational P²/(linear P). Let me check each quickly.

### Candidate 47: Set c5=0, c3=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t)`. Missing rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 48: Set c3=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c5*exp(c6*t)*log(P*c7+1)`. exp*log term is transcendental. Set c5=0: missing rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 49: Set c3=0, c5=0: missing rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 50: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*log(P*c4+1) + c5*exp(c6/P)`
Set c5=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*log(P*c4+1)`. log ≠ rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 51: Set c3=0, c5=0: missing rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 52: Set c3=0, c5=0: missing rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 53: Set c3=0: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + c5*t*(P+c6)^c7`. Has t dependence in non-exp term. Set c5=0: missing rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 54: Set c3=0, c5=0: missing rational. **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 55: `P²*c0 + P²*c1 + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4 + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*t+1)+c8)`
Set c5=0: same as Candidate 10/11 without rational term. `P²*(c0+c1) + P*c2*exp(c3*t) + P*c4`. No rational P²/(linear P). **[NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 56: `P*c0 + P*c1*exp(c2*t) + P*c3*log(1+c4/P)`
P*c3*log(1+c4/P) is transcendental, not rational. **[NO MATCH]**
